[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run of the `html` binary [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpart of libxml2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m under AddressSanitizer has [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrevealed a heap-buffer-overflow in the function `htmlSecureComment` within [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HTMLparser.c`. During processing of a malformed comment in an HTML document, a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memcpy` invocation writes beyond the bounds of a heap-allocated buffer by [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes, triggering an ASan abort.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The AddressSanitizer report indicates a multi-byte write overflow on the heap. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSpecifically, a call to `__asan_memcpy` in `htmlSecureComment` overruns a [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion by writing [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m bytes past its end.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is classified as a heap-buffer-overflow, where data is written beyond the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region in memory.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The overflow occurs at `HTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3591:13[0m[39m` inside `htmlSecureComment`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalled by `htmlTopParseComment`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The buffer in question is allocated via `xmlFuzzMalloc` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwrapper around [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`malloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at `fuzz.[0m[1;92mc:127[0m[39m` for use in comment processing.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The ASan output shows the allocated region spans addresses [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x515000000580[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and the overflow write begins exactly at the end[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof that region.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The stack trace demonstrates the path through the fuzzing harness [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzz/html.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into the HTML parsing routines.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `htmlSecureComment` and its surrounding logic in `HTMLparser.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3335[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m3591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The buffer allocation in `xmlFuzzMalloc` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/fuzz.[0m[1;92mc:127[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and its interaction [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the secure comment routine  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Callers of `htmlSecureComment`, particularly `htmlTopParseComment` and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhigher-level functions like `htmlParseDocument` and `htmlCtxtParseDocument`  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzing harness entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz/html.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to understand how input is fed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the parsing functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough the harness itself is not the root cause[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwas attempted to fix the overflow by tightening the resizing condition—changing the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check to `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m parses HTML input via [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment` in HTMLparser.c.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - AddressSanitizer reports a heap-buffer-overflow: a [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m-byte write at the end [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof a [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte region.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The backtrace shows the overflow occurs in `__asan_memcpy` called from [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment`, indicating that the temporary buffer allocated for comment [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrewriting is too small for the data being copied.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations from the ASan Log  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The faulty write is from `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer + used, chunk, chunkSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimilar for `repl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where the buffer was not grown to hold `used + chunkSize + [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplSize`.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The buffer was originally allocated via `xmlFuzzMalloc` and its size tracked [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `buffer_size`.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No guard existed to ensure `buffer_size >= used + extraSize` before copying.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Target file: libxml2’s HTMLparser.c, around line [0m[1;36m3574[0m[39m.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original code snippet [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapproximate[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         chunkSize = in - chunk;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand duplicated buffer assignments.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
